--
-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `prpagdefn`
--

CREATE TABLE `prpagdefn` (
  `pagnombre` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 NOT NULL,
  `version` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `camposcont` smallint(6) DEFAULT NULL,
  `gridhoriz` smallint(6) DEFAULT NULL,
  `gridvertical` smallint(6) DEFAULT NULL,
  `helpcontextnum` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `paneltop` smallint(6) DEFAULT NULL,
  `panelleft` smallint(6) DEFAULT NULL,
  `panelright` smallint(6) DEFAULT NULL,
  `panelbottom` smallint(6) DEFAULT NULL,
  `pnlstyle` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `stylesheetname` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `descripcion` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `popupmenu` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `ultima_actualizacion` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `ultimo_oprid` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `propietario` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `lenguaje_cd` varchar(3) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `linkpag` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

--
-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `sys_config`
--

CREATE TABLE `sys_config` (
  `cid` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sysappname` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `sysappver` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `notify_oncreate` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `notify_onupdate` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `notify_ondelete` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `show_publiccal` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `expinfo_status` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `expinfo_guestname` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `expinfo_guestnum` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `expinfo_guestcountry` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `expinfo_remarks` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `expinfo_pptaddress` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `publiccal_view` tinyint(3) DEFAULT NULL,
  `publiccal_urlonly` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `sysdeflanguage` varchar(5) DEFAULT NULL,
  `sysuicorners` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0'
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

--
-- Volcado de datos para la tabla `sys_config`
--

  `importance` enum('yes','no') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'no'
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ROW_FORMAT=DYNAMIC;

--
-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `sys_mailtemplates`
--

CREATE TABLE `sys_mailtemplates` (
  `id` int(5) NOT NULL,
  `name_en` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `subject_en` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `subject_ms` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `subject_fr` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `subject_it` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `subject_pt` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `subject_nl` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `subject_es` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `subject_de` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `help_en` text,
  `body_en` text,
  `body_ms` text,
  `body_fr` text,
  `body_it` text,
  `body_pt` text,
  `body_nl` text,
  `body_es` text,
  `body_de` text,
  `type` enum('news','mailer') DEFAULT 'mailer',
  `typeid` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ROW_FORMAT=DYNAMIC;

--

--
-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `sys_users`
--

CREATE TABLE `sys_users` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `username` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(60) NOT NULL,
  `fname` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `token` varchar(40) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `userlevel` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `created` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `lastlogin` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `lastip` varchar(16) DEFAULT '0',
  `access` text,
  `notes` tinytext,
  `info` tinytext,
  `active` enum('y','n','t','b') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'n',
  `company` varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL,
  `cphone` varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL,
  `caddress` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `akey` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `pptassignment` text
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ROW_FORMAT=DYNAMIC;

--
-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `tbl_abonos_reservas`
--

CREATE TABLE `tbl_abonos_reservas` (
  `setid` varchar(3) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `id_reserva` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8 NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `seq_abono` varchar(5) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `id_tipo_pago` varchar(5) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `fecha_pago` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `valor_pago` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `moneda_cd` varchar(5) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `base_pago` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `impto_pago` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_deposito` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_pago` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `numer_rec` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `numero_fact` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `cod_banco` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `num_cuenta` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `num_ref` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `val_desc` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `estado` varchar(3) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `adiciona_fecha` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `ultimo_oprid` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `ultima_actualizacion` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_cliente` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_tercero` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_registro` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `saldo` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `valor_abono` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `valor_porc` double DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Estructura de tabla para la tabla `tbl_det_reservas`
--

CREATE TABLE `tbl_det_reservas` (
  `seq_numero` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `setid` varchar(3) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `id_reserva` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8 NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `id_tipo_serv` varchar(5) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_habitacion` varchar(5) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `fecha_ini` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `fecha_checkin` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `fecha_fin` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `fecha_checkout` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `idtipotarifa` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `cant_adultos` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `estado` varchar(30) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `adiciona_fecha` timestamp NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `ultimo_oprid` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `ultima_actualizacion` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_tipo_hab` varchar(5) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_mobiliario` varchar(3) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_tercero` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_tipo_pago` varchar(3) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `cantidad` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `cant_menores` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `moneda_cd` varchar(3) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
  `ajapues` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `canal` varchar(5) DEFAULT NULL,
  `asesor` varchar(5) DEFAULT NULL,
  `parqueadero` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `tipovehiculo` varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL,
  `placa` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `note` varchar(150) DEFAULT NULL,
  `desayuno` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0'
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

CREATE TABLE `tbl_tarifas` (
  `setid` varchar(3) CHARACTER SET utf8 NOT NULL,
  `idtipotarifa` varchar(5) CHARACTER SET utf8 NOT NULL,
  `idtipohab` varchar(5) CHARACTER SET utf8 NOT NULL,
  `descripcion` varchar(150) CHARACTER SET utf8 NOT NULL,
  `tarifa` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `estado` varchar(1) CHARACTER SET utf8 DEFAULT NULL,
